Purchase options are available for continuing to use the App after the trial is over.\r\n \r\nUltra Office Suite is a comprehensive office suite for viewing and editing a wide range of documents. Not only can it support Microsoft Office file formats like Word, Excel, and PowerPoint but also OpenOffice document files. Plus, it also offers a vector graphics and flowcharts drawing program, a databases editor, and a Math formula editing application.\r\n\r\n*** File formats Ultra Office Suite can open\r\nUltra Office
